< review>
Amazing LITTLE place. A perfect example of a wonderful "hole in the wall" restaurant!! The staff was very cheery and eager to help and suggest items. The food came in HUGE portions!!! And was definitely under priced. The seating was limited to about 6 tables as it was raining outside. But they accommodated everyone and it was a pleasure eating there. Will most definitely go back!!!</review>

< text>
We wanted a more casual evening as part of a recent trip to Guernville and this placed seemed to fit the bill.  Both my wife and I had BBQ, me the pulled pork sandwich and she just had the pork plate (same basic concept, but since she's gluten free, it skips the bun).  We sat in the outside dining area, which, with the heaters on, was just about perfect (other than a little road noise).  They had some decent beers (in bottles) and the BBQ was well done.  My wife really enjoyed the sweet potato fries.  Pleasant dinner at a very reasonable price, with solid service.< /text>

<Text>I heard of this place by ear. It is quit cozy. They serve Taylor Maid coffee which made me sit. I love a nice cup of coffee with my breakfast. Rarely, do I ever encounter good food, AND good coffee. We order our food to which the waitress repeated correctly. I may add they were busy; one of our extra request was not fullfilled. We asked for a plate to go. When our food came, it was ok. My bacon and potatoes were cold. Eggs were perfect. I liked the spicey Bloody Mary.  I would have LOVED it with less horse raddish. (My bartending teacher said," You can make enemies if you add too much horse raddish.") I am particular with my food, and I look forward to each meal, but I will never be too harsh if I'm disappointed. However, I decided to point out an obvious harsh mistake, it could be just an eyesore. I noticed the waitress making up a few drinks for the table next to ours. I wanted to see how they fixed their drinks. I did not expect genuine ingredients to go in the drinks.  I couldn't dismiss the tray of drinks were placed on top of the garbage can. I don't care how clean the can could be, I just think this was a bad mistake. I am grateful for a nice meal I don't have to cook. This is a reminder to the staff to always follow the food and safety handlers' rules.< /Text>< pictures>

I have been taking my vehicles to Firestone Auto care for years and this review is long overdue. I have always received excellent service from Firstone both in Clovis and Fresno locations as well as by phone. The front desk staff are always friendly and professional. Guillermo is the store manager at the location on West Shaw in Fresno and treats me like a personal guest and is very thorough. He takes the time to answer all my questions regarding the diagnostics and assessments of my vehicle. Remembers to apply every discount possible to my bill, and makes time to do quick checks on my car if i come in short notice because an indicator light came on in my dash. This was my first time at this breakfast (also has lunch) restaurant. I would rate this place at 4.5 stars compared to other kinds of Dinner's; Food was big portions, tasted good, server was very honest not trying to oversell, seemed like a home vibe because of the employees attitudes.  The cons are the ambiance, and the seats are needing a remodel. Not bad for a true dinner; I feel that pros outweigh the cons. Ate lunch here today with a friend.

The staff was very friendly. She took our drink order right away...and then the order. We did not have to wait very long..I had a groupon... that's what brought me in.

I ordered the cowboy burger. The bacon was crispy...it came with bbq sauce on the side...and onion rings.  Lettuce..tomato..pickles.

The burger was so good... the fries crispy.  I would certainly come back here to eat again...< /Review>

< review>
Best place to get breakfast in the entire north Sacramento area. I go in once a week maybe for a large breakfast. My food always comes out fast and hot and it tastes great. Wait staff is friendly and always on point. The main cook even came out and sat with me one time and made me feel appreciated just because he noticed I'd been in there a few times. Also need to mention you get a good amount of food for the price compared to any other restaurants in the area. The furniture is old and some things in the place need replacement or maintenance for sure but it's otherwise clean and comfortable. Eat here.<//review>

<rating>5<//rating>< Text>
Family owned and operated (hands on) since 1977. Extra friendly, fast service with attentive staff that included on our visit two of the family members in full swing helping us enjoy a great meal. One was our waitress, who was excellent and we met her brother who was in the kitchen (he personally delivered a steak to me that I had sent back because it was a little under cooked for me, he was apologetic and they even discounted my order because of it, I was very impressed with the customer service) Large menu with everything a breakfast appetite could ask for including Eggs Benedict in various presentations, huge 4 egg omelettes, steak and eggs with hash browns or country fries, lots and lots more. Not the newest building or the latest decor but you will find a place that might be your go to place for very good food and service.</Text>

<Review>I'll get into why I gave this place 3 stars in a minute, but first I wanna say the service here was excellent. Very attentive and friendly staff.
When it comes to the food, it was OK. My boyfriend ordered an omelet with hash browns. I ordered blueberry pancakes with eggs. I enjoyed my bf's meal much more than my own. The omelet was delicious, and if I ever go back that is what I will order. My pancakes were a little gummy and my eggs were flavorless. All they would have to do is add salt and pepper and I'm sure my eggs would have been much better.
Lastly, the worst part of my experience was the atmosphere on the inside. From the outside, Eggies looks like a cute little retro diner. But on the inside, man can it use some renovation! The side of the restaurant in which we were seated was dark, gloomy, and the carpet was dirty. The booths look like they were about to fall apart. The chairs are miss matched. < Review>
Food is pretty good. Prices are high. Chicken Fried steak and coffee costs over $20. They only take cash now no cards. I can only assume the owner didn't like paying the 2-4% and hassle of merchant services but I never carry cash anymore. I walked in once a month ago and left because I didn't have the cash. Provise an ATM at little cost on site rather than the gas station across the street that charges 3.50.  Unfortunately this decision is costing them business. I like seeing long term small business doing well but I really question this choice.

In short food is good, prices are high. Get the Groupon online<//Review>

<review>Good thing I had a coupon!

The buscuits weren't really buscuits, they were cut from a sheet of baked dough. They were dry and bland. The srambled eggs were done well but that's not saying much. I've never smoked so it can't be blamed on dulled taste buds.

I am a fanatic about southern breakfast and have had many exceptional ones in my day-this goes down as exceptionally awful. Its a shame really because I live across the street and was thrilled that there was an american diner right on my doorstep. Sigh 65$ for a whole lot of leftovers that I had to fix when I got home by making my own country gravy!
